msg:It's very close to the Science and Technology Museum, about ten minutes' walk away, and the Bird's Nest is not far away either. It's very convenient to go for a walk by bicycle at night. It was booked to facilitate a one-day trip to the Science and Technology Museum, and the rest is really hard to describe.
The first room I was given was at the end of the corridor. As soon as I entered, I saw a connecting door. The child next door happened to be crying. The sound insulation was too poor, so I asked to change rooms. Someone at the front desk quickly came up and gave us the room card for another room and took us there. When we opened the door, the child asked why there were two peepholes. I hadn't noticed it yet. When I entered, I found that the bathroom was very spacious and it was barrier-free. It was so emotional. For wheelchair convenience. We asked to change again, and after waiting for a while this time, they came to take us to another normal room at the end of the corridor. There were no children crying. It was just that the light was on as soon as the door was opened. It was obvious that dust was floating in the air. We were tired after all the tossing. If you want to wash up and rest early, just make do with it. Unexpectedly, I woke up the next morning and saw a huge human-shaped black shadow on the ceiling. I was so scared that I almost cried. My husband said it was the shadow on the ceiling. When I calmed down, it seemed different from what I saw at first. Same. . .
Breakfast is included. I went a little late on the first day, half an hour before lunch ended. There was no choice, and the wontons didn't look too cooked. It was okay if I went before eight o'clock the next day. I could eat enough, but it wasn't a rich meal.
There are many places to eat nearby, with various flavors. It's just okay. I wouldn't recommend it to friends who want to go to the science and technology museum.

Because it is not a family hotel, the software and hardware are a bit simple compared to other five-star resort hotels. After staying for three consecutive nights, the hotel provided a breakfast of normal quality.
To sum up, as an old five-star hotel, the price/performance ratio is moderate, the lobby is very stylish, the room decoration can be renovated, and the service level is online. I originally wanted to give it 4.2 stars, but because of the thoughtfulness of the beautiful and handsome guys at the front desk, I can give it 4.5 stars.

name:W‍e‍n‍j‍i‍n‍g‍J‍a‍v‍e‍l‍i‍n
info:Superior Queen Room
info:Stayed in July 2023
info:Family
info:35 Reviews
rating:3.2
posted:Posted July 20, 2023
msg:I used to pass by the hotel every day to and from get off work, but I didn't expect to have the opportunity to stay here after so long. My impression of Marco Polo has always been good, but unfortunately this time the experience was not so good.

Let’s talk about the hardware facilities first. In fact, the overall environment and conditions are pretty good, but old is a flaw. After all, many things are old, so they don’t look so high-end and fashionable.

The bed is still very comfortable, which is very important, but the bed may have been made in a hurry, and it doesn't feel as neat as I do at home.

The bathroom has a shower room and a bathtub. The shower is only hand-held and has no overhead spray. The hot water is really hot, but unfortunately, when the water temperature is adjusted to an appropriate level, the water flow is not good. The washbasin is slightly smaller, and the bathtub, toilet, washbasin, etc. are all American standard configurations.

The swimming pool and gym are located on the 4th floor. The swimming pool looks more like a space for children to entertain. There are no professional swimming lanes. The depth is 1.5m, and the sides are relatively shallow. If there are a little more people, it may not be suitable. By the way, the short-haired lady and staff I met at the front desk of the fitness space are really super nice.

The dissatisfaction this time is mainly at the front desk when checking in. I can only say that some young front desk staff still need more training, lack of experience, and insufficient adaptability. When serving in the hotel, they may encounter all kinds of tricky guests. This kind of handling is really terrible.

I won't name the girls at the front desk. In case of emergencies, the guests have already expressed their dissatisfaction. There are no professional words, no polite apology, and no reasonable solution, only vague and perfunctory. Even in the process of successfully checking in later, there was almost an operation of overcharging. There is no mention of the elevator instructions, the location and time of breakfast, whether parking is required, and other relevant information and guidance. The more flustered the situation, the more the test of basic skills, girl, you have to work harder.

msg:遇到了奇葩遭遇。
1.11月初入住房間悶熱無比，關掉空調依然是桑拿房，房間內的空調説冬天不能製冷，孩子熱到半後夜不睡
2.房間窗户衹能叫服務員開關。自己沒辦法控制。
3.房間硬件很差，特別是淋雨。淅淅瀝瀝的淋浴頭出水效果
4.房間的燈控也沒有明確標識
5.早餐豆漿一股發酵味，介於豆漿和豆汁之間的味道，服務人員説就是這個味道沒問題。當我沒喝過豆漿....早餐的食材明顯不新鮮，沙拉吧的胡蘿絲和青菜葉都是枯萎的，明顯是隔夜菜。種類也很少，品質差！
6.晚上睡覺忘記反鎖，早上6點多房間門被兩個男人打開，説服務員做錯房卡了，孩子嚇得哇哇大哭。

千萬千萬千萬不要住這個酒店。
住了絕對會後悔！
